/* use whatever your normal bin height is */\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n# ✅ Fix 2 — Make HM03 Red + Side Bin\n\nAdd:\n\n```css\n/* Side bins */\n.side-bin {\n    border-left: 4px solid #c40000;\n}\n\n/* Highlight HM03 */\n#HM03 {\n    background-color: #c40000;\n    color: white;\n}\n```\n\nMake sure HM03 has both classes:\n\n```html\n<div class=\"bin hm-wide hm-bin side-bin\" id=\"HM03\" style=\"grid-column:1/-1;\">\n```\n\n---\n\n# ✅ Fix 3 — Every 6th Bin After HM03 is Side Bin\n\nIf your numbering continues normally (H06, H12, H18, etc.), and you want automatic alignment:\n\nAdd this CSS:\n\n```css\n/* Every 6th bin globally aligned as side bin */\n.h-hh-container .bin:nth-child(6n) {\n    border-left: 4px solid #c40000;\n}\n```\n\nIf you only want this behavior inside H and HH (not HM), use:\n\n```css\n.h-hh-container .bin:not(.hm-bin):nth-child(6n) {\n    border-left: 4px solid #c40000;\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n# ✅ Fix 4 — Keep Side Bins in Perfect Vertical Line\n\nBecause this is CSS Grid, alignment depends on consistent row height.\n\nForce consistent height:\n\n```css\n.h-hh-container .bin {\n    display:flex;\n    align-items:center;\n    justify-content:center;\n    box-sizing:border-box;\n}\n```\n\nIf alignment is still slightly off, remove any internal margin/padding differences between `.hh-bin`, `.hm-bin`, and normal `.bin`.\n\n---\n\n# Result Will Be\n\nH02 | HH02  \nH03 | HH03  \nH04 | HH04  \n\nHM01  \nHM02  \nHM03  ← red + side  \nHM04  \n\nH05 | HH05  \nH06 | HH06  ← side  \nH07 | HH07  \nH08 | HH08  \nH09 | HH09  \nH10 | HH10  \nH11 | HH11  \nH12 | HH12  ← side  \n\nEverything vertically aligned.\n\n---\n\nIf you want, I can regenerate the corrected file with these spacing + highlight fixes baked in cleanly so you don’t have to edit manually."

should literally behave like:\n\n```\nH02 | HH02\nH03 | HH03\nH04 | HH04\n\nHM01  (full width)\nHM02  (full width)\nHM03  (full width)\nHM04  (full width)\n\nH05 | HH05\nH06 | HH06\n```\n\nThat means:\n\n• Keep H and HH as two columns  \n• Insert 4 full-width grid rows between row 04 and 05  \n• Each HM bin spans BOTH columns  \n• No flex tricks  \n• No fake rows  \n\nThis is a proper CSS Grid job.\n\n---\n\n# ✅ The Correct Structural Fix\n\nYou need to convert `.h-hh-container` into a **2-column grid** where each row is aligned across both columns.\n\n---\n\n## 1️⃣ Update the container CSS\n\nReplace your current `.h-hh-container` CSS with this:\n\n```css\n.h-hh-container {\n    display: grid;\n    grid-template-columns: 1fr 120px; /* H column | HH column */\n    gap: 6px 12px;\n    align-items: start;\n}\n```\n\nRemove any `display:flex` from `.h-hh-container`.\n\n---\n\n## 2️⃣ Flatten H and HH columns\n\nInside `.h-hh-container`, remove the `.h-col` and `.hh-col` wrappers entirely.\n\nInstead of:\n\n```html\n<div class=\"h-col\">\n   H02\n   H03\n</div>\n\n<div class=\"hh-col\">\n   HH02\n   HH03\n</div>\n```\n\nYou want the bins directly inside the grid container.\n\n---\n\n## 3️⃣ Correct HTML Structure (This is what it should look like)\n\nInside `.h-hh-container`, structure it exactly like this:\n\n```html\n<div class=\"h-hh-container\">\n\n    <!-- Row 02 -->\n    <div class=\"bin\"><div class=\"bin-id\">H02</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">16</div></div>\n    <div class=\"bin hh-bin\"><div class=\"bin-id\">HH02</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">5</div></div>\n\n    <!-- Row 03 -->\n    <div class=\"bin\"><div class=\"bin-id\">H03</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">16</div></div>\n    <div class=\"bin hh-bin\"><div class=\"bin-id\">HH03</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">5</div></div>\n\n    <!-- Row 04 -->\n    <div class=\"bin\"><div class=\"bin-id\">H04</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">16</div></div>\n    <div class=\"bin hh-bin\"><div class=\"bin-id\">HH04</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">5</div></div>\n\n    <!-- HM FULL WIDTH SECTION -->\n    <div class=\"bin hm-wide hm-bin\" style=\"grid-column: 1 / -1;\">\n        <div class=\"bin-id\">HM01</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">22</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"bin hm-wide hm-bin\" style=\"grid-column: 1 / -1;\">\n        <div class=\"bin-id\">HM02</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">22</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"bin hm-wide hm-bin side-bin\" style=\"grid-column: 1 / -1;\">\n        <div class=\"bin-id\">HM03</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">6</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <div class=\"bin hm-wide hm-bin\" style=\"grid-column: 1 / -1;\">\n        <div class=\"bin-id\">HM04</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">20</div>\n    </div>\n\n    <!-- Row 05 -->\n    <div class=\"bin\"><div class=\"bin-id\">H05</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">16</div></div>\n    <div class=\"bin hh-bin\"><div class=\"bin-id\">HH05</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">5</div></div>\n\n    <!-- Row 06 -->\n    <div class=\"bin\"><div class=\"bin-id\">H06</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">19</div></div>\n    <div class=\"bin hh-bin\"><div class=\"bin-id\">HH06</div><div class=\"bin-capacity\">5</div></div>\n\n</div>\n```\n\n---\n\n# 🔥 Why This Works\n\nCSS Grid auto-places items in rows:\n\n- First item → column 1\n- Second item → column 2\n- Third item → next row column 1\n- Fourth → next row column 2\n\nWhen you add:\n\n```\ngrid-column: 1 / -1;\n```\n\nThat element spans across both columns — creating a full-width row.\n\nNo hacks. No wrappers. No splitting. No reflow problems.\n\n---\n\n# ⚠️ Important\n\nIf you keep the `.h-col` and `.hh-col` wrappers, this will never align correctly.\n\nThe grid must control row pairing directly.\n\n---\n\nIf you want, I can now regenerate a corrected full HTML file from your uploaded version with this exact structure properly implemented end-to-end."
